Worst-case          probability of this event, for a 900k block, is about          2.0e-3 for 32 bits, 1.0e-5 for 40 bits and 4.0e-8 for 48 bits.          For a compressed file of size 100Gb -- about 100000 blocks --          only a 48-bit marker will do.  NB: normal compression/          decompression do *not* rely on these statistical properties.          They are only important when trying to recover blocks from          damaged files.        */	WITHOUT_CLASSIFICATION	0.9999999998635503	WITHOUT_CLASSIFICATION	1.3644965490611688E-10	TEST
